A series of paintings about her mother's daily life, such as cooking in the kitchen, braiding children's hair and doing housework, are now displayed at the local cultural center.;一系列关于她母亲日常生活的画作，如在厨房做饭，给孩子的头发编辫子和做家务，现在都在当地的文化中心展出。
